Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-25 11:29:50]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to

				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment

				, cms_quotation.created_date

				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

{"client_id":"","created_by":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 12:39:03]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-25 14:55:49]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-25 14:59:00]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: get_quotation_list

{"client_id":"","created_by":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 15:03:33]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-25 15:05:34]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.status_id in(187) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.status_id in(188) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-25 16:14:56]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-25 17:00:31]
Function Details: get_quotation_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 17:00:31]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-25 17:30:36]
Function Details: get_quotation_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 17:30:36]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

[2018-11-25 19:25:39]
Function Details: get_quotation_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":10,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 19:25:39]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 10,10

				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 10,10

                 FROM 
                cms_quotation

                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: get_quotation_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 19:43:52]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_quotation.attention_to

Function Details: get_quotation_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 21:55:39]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 22:58:40]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: get_quotation_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 23:04:23]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: get_quotation_list 
 Param Details : 
{"client_id":"","created_by":"","category_id":"","status_id":"","view_all":"0","start_index":0,"limit":10,"is_admin":"0","emp_id":"15"}


[2018-11-25 23:17:10]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

				, cms_quotation.attention_to

Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10

SELECT cms_document_archiving.doc_no
				, cms_document_archiving.doc_date
				, cms_document_archiving.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_document_archiving.from_date
				, cms_document_archiving.to_date
				, IF(cms_document_archiving.notify = 1, 'Yes','No') as notify
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_by
				, cms_document_archiving.notify_email
				, cms_document_archiving.attachment
				, cms_document_archiving.remarks
				, cms_document_archiving.approvals
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.doc_type) as doc_type
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_document_archiving.status_id) as status_name
				, cms_document_archiving.created_date
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_document_archiving.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_document_archiving
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_document_archiving.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_document_archiving.created_by) AND cms_document_archiving.is_active in(1) ORDER BY doc_no DESC limit 0,10

Function Details: get_quotation_list 
 Param Details :

[2018-11-25 23:40:26]
Function Details: db_query_list
 Param Details: 
SELECT cms_quotation.quote_no
				, cms_quotation.quote_date
				, cms_quotation.client_id
				, IFNULL(cms_clients.name,'') as client_name
				, cms_quotation.attention_to
				, cms_quotation.email_content
				, cms_quotation.email
				, cms_quotation.attachment
				, cms_quotation.remarks
				, cms_quotation.approvals
				, cms_quotation.created_date
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.ctg_id) as category_name
				, (select descr from cms_master_list list where list.id = cms_quotation.status_id) as status_name
				, (select name from cms_employees emp where emp.id = cms_quotation.created_by) as created_by		
                 FROM 
                cms_quotation
				LEFT JOIN cms_clients
                    ON (cms_quotation.client_id = cms_clients.id)
                 WHERE 15 IN (cms_quotation.created_by) AND cms_quotation.is_active in(1) ORDER BY quote_no DESC limit 0,10
